				limit = { check_variable = { free_trait_picks > 0 } }
				add_to_variable = { free_trait_picks = -1 }
			}
			else = {
				FROM = { small_expenditure = yes }
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = { FROM.interest_rate > 8 }
			}
		}
	}

}
